                def act(world_state)
          
      35. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    35. 
            

            

                  return default_action unless @alive && process_alive?
          
      36.

      37.

                  begin
          
      38.

                    # Send world state to agent

                  rescue Timeout::Error

                    Mutation.logger.warn("Agent #{@agent_id} timed out, using default action")
          
      60. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    60. 
            

            

                    default_action
          
      61. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    61. 
            

            

                  rescue JSON::ParserError => e

                def kill_process
          
      72.

                  return unless @pid
          
      73.

                  begin

                    if process_alive?

      86.

                        sleep(0.1)
          
      91.

                      end

    92. 
            

            

                    end

                def format_neighbors(neighbors)
          
      219.

                  directions = ['north_west', 'north', 'north_east', 'west', 'east', 'south_west', 'south', 'south_east']

                  result = {}

                          energy: 0,

                    # neighbors is an array

                      direction = directions[index]
          
      242. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    242. 
            

            

                      if neighbor && neighbor.respond_to?(:energy)
          
      243.

                        result[direction] = {
          
      244.

                          energy: neighbor.energy,

                def update_viewport

                  # Clamp camera position to valid ranges

      70.

                private

                def display_loop
          
      93. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    93. 
            

            

                  frame_time = 1.0 / @display_fps
          
      94. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    94. 
            

            

                  
          
      95. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    95. 
            

            

                  while @running
          
      96. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    96. 
            

            

                    frame_start = Time.now
          
      97. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    97. 
            

            

                    
          
      98. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    98. 
            

            

                    begin
          
      99. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    99. 
            

            

                      # Check for input first (OS buffers keypresses)
          
      100. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    100. 
            

            

                      handle_input
          
      101. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    101. 
            

            

                      
          
      102. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    102. 
            

            

                      # Exit immediately if quit was pressed
          
      103. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    103. 
            

            

                      break unless @running
          
      104. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    104. 
            

            

            
          
      105. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    105. 
            

            

                      # Step the simulation based on its own timing
          
      106. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    106. 
            

            

                      step_simulation_with_timing
          
      107. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    107. 
            

            

            
          
      108. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    108. 
            

            

                      # Exit immediately if quit was pressed during simulation step
          
      109. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    109. 
            

            

                      break unless @running
          
      110. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    110. 
            

            

            
          
      111. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    111. 
            

            

                      # Update display
          
      112. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    112. 
            

            

                      draw_world
          
      113. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    113. 
            

            

                      draw_status_bar
          
      114. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    114. 
            

            

                      draw_help
          
      115. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    115. 
            

            

                      Curses.refresh
          
      116. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    116. 
            

            

            
          
      117. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    117. 
            

            

                      # Track FPS
          
      118. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    118. 
            

            

                      @frame_count += 1
          
      119. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    119. 
            

            

            
          
      120. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    120. 
            

            

                      # Check for terminal resize
          
      121. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    121. 
            

            

                      check_terminal_resize
          
      122. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    122. 
            

            

            
          
      123. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    123. 
            

            

                      # Sleep to maintain target FPS
          
      124. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    124. 
            

            

                      frame_elapsed = Time.now - frame_start
          
      125. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    125. 
            

            

                      sleep_time = frame_time - frame_elapsed
          
      126. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    126. 
            

            

                      sleep(sleep_time) if sleep_time > 0
          
      127. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    127. 
            

            

                    rescue StandardError => e
          
      128. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    128. 
            

            

                      # Log error but continue running unless we're trying to quit
          
      129. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    129. 
            

            

                      Mutation.logger.debug("Display error: #{e.message}")
          
      130. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    130. 
            

            

                      break unless @running  # Exit if we're quitting, even on error
          
      131. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    131. 
            

            

                      sleep(0.01)
          
      132. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    132. 
            

            

                    end
          
      133. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    133. 
            

            

                  end
          
      134. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    134. 
            

            

                end
          
      135. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    135. 
            

            

            
          
      136. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    136. 
            
              1
            

            

                def step_simulation
          
      137. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    137. 
            

            

                  return if @paused
          
      138. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    138. 
            

            

                  return unless @simulator
          
      139. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    139. 
            

            

                  return unless @running # Stop stepping if quit was pressed
          
      140. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    140. 
            

            

            
          
      141. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    141. 
            

            

                  @simulator.step

                def step_simulation_with_timing
          
      145. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    145. 
            

            

                  return if @paused
          
      146. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    146. 
            

            

                  return unless @simulator
          
      147. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    147. 
            

            

                  return unless @running # Stop stepping if quit was pressed
          
      148. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    148. 
            

            

            
          
      149. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    149. 
            

            

                  current_time = Time.now
          
      150. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    150. 
            

            

                  simulation_delay = Mutation.configuration.simulation_delay
          
      151. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    151. 
            

            

                  
          
      152. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    152. 
            

            

                  # Only step if enough time has passed since last step
          
      153. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    153. 
            

            

                  if current_time - @last_step_time >= simulation_delay
          
      154. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    154. 
            

            

                    @simulator.step
          
      155. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    155. 
            

            

                    @last_step_time = current_time
          
      156. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    156. 
            

            

                  end
          
      157. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    157. 
            

            

                end
          
      158. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    158. 
            

            

            
          
      159. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    159. 
            
              1
            

            

                def calculate_fps
          
      160. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    160. 
            

            

                  current_time = Time.now
          
      161. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    161. 
            

            

                  elapsed = current_time - @fps_start_time
          
      162. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    162. 
            

            

                  
          
      163. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    163. 
            

            

                  # Update FPS every second
          
      164. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    164. 
            

            

                  if elapsed >= 1.0
          
      165. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    165. 
            

            

                    fps = (@frame_count / elapsed).round(1)
          
      166. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    166. 
            

            

                    @frame_count = 0
          
      167. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    167. 
            

            

                    @fps_start_time = current_time
          
      168. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    168. 
            

            

                    @current_fps = fps
          
      169. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    169. 
            

            

                  end
          
      170. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    170. 
            

            

                  
          
      171. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    171. 
            

            

                  @current_fps || 0.0
          
      172. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    172. 
            

            

                end
          
      173. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    173. 
            

            

            
          
      174. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    174. 
            
              1
            

            

                def handle_input
          
      175. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    175. 
            

            

                  # Use curses timeout for non-blocking input
          
      176.

                  Curses.stdscr.timeout = 0 # Non-blocking
          
      177. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    177. 
            

            

                  key = Curses.getch
          
      178. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    178. 
            

            

                  input_received = false
          
      179. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    179. 
            

            

            
          
      180. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    180. 
            

            

                  if key && key != -1
          
      181. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    181. 
            

            

                    
          
      182. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    182. 
            

            

                    input_received = true

    183. 
            

            

                    @last_key = begin

                    rescue StandardError

                    end

      189. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    189. 
            

            

                    case key
          
      190.

                    when 'q', 'Q'
          
      191. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    191. 
            

            

                      @running = false

    194. 
            

            

                      @simulator&.request_quit

                    when ' ' # Space for pause/resume

                      @paused = !@paused

                      @last_key = @paused ? 'PAUSED' : 'RESUMED'

                      # Force immediate display update to show pause state
          
      199. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    199. 
            

            

                      draw_world
          
      200. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    200. 
            

            

                      draw_status_bar
          
      201. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    201. 
            

            

                      draw_help
          
      202. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    202. 
            

            

                      Curses.refresh
          
      203. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    203. 
            

            

                    when 'w', 'W'
          
      204. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    204. 
            

            

                      move_camera(0, -1)
          
      205. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    205. 
            

            

                      @last_key = 'UP'
          
      206. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    206. 
            

            

                      # Force immediate display update to show camera movement
          
      207. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    207. 
            

            

                      draw_world
          
      208. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    208. 
            

            

                      draw_status_bar
          
      209. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    209. 
            

            

                      draw_help

                      Curses.refresh

                    when 's', 'S'

                      move_camera(0, 1)

                      @last_key = 'DOWN'
          
      214.

                      # Force immediate display update to show camera movement
          
      215. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    215. 
            

            

                      draw_world

                      draw_status_bar

                      # Force immediate display update to show camera movement

                      # Force immediate display update to show camera movement

      69. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    69. 
            

            

                    executable = @agent_executables.sample # Random executable
          
      70. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    70. 
            

            

                    
          
      71. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    71. 
            

            

                    agent = @agent_manager.spawn_agent(
          
      72. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    72. 
            

            

                      executable, x, y, 
          
      73. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    73. 
            

            

                      Mutation.configuration.initial_energy, 
          
      74. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    74. 
            

            

                      @generation + 1
          
      75. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    75. 
            

            

                    )
          
      76. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    76. 
            

            

                    
          
      77. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    77. 
            

            

                    if agent
          
      78. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    78. 
            

            

                      @grid[y][x] = agent
          
      79. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    79. 
            

            

                      @statistics[:total_agents_created] += 1
          
      80. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    80. 
            

            

                    end
          
      81. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    81. 
            

            

                  end
          
      82. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    82. 
            

            

            
          
      83. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    83. 
            

            

                  @generation += 1
          
      84. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    84. 
            

            

                  @statistics[:total_generations] = @generation
          
      85. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    85. 
            

            

            
          
      86. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    86. 
            

            

                  Mutation.logger.generation("🌱 Generation #{@generation} seeded with #{living_agents.count} agents (#{coverage_percentage}% of #{@width}x#{@height})")
          
      87. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    87. 
            

            

                end
          
      88. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    88. 
            

            

            
          
      89. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    89. 
            
              1
            

            

                def step
          
      90. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    90. 
            

            

                  # Build individual world states for each agent including their neighbors
          
      91. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    91. 
            

            

                  agent_world_states = {}
          
      92. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    92. 
            

            

                  
          
      93. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    93. 
            

            

                  @grid.each_with_index do |row, y|
          
      94. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    94. 
            

            

                    row.each_with_index do |agent, x|
          
      95. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    95. 
            

            

                      next unless agent&.alive
          
      96. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    96. 
            

            

            
          
      97. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    97. 
            

            

                      # Get neighbors for this specific agent
          
      98. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    98. 
            

            

                      neighbors = get_neighbors(x, y)
          
      99. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    99. 
            

            

                      
          
      100. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    100. 
            

            

                      agent_world_states[agent.agent_id] = {
          
      101. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    101. 
            

            

                        tick: @tick,
          
      102. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    102. 
            

            

                        world_size: [@width, @height],
          
      103. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    103. 
            

            

                        timeout_ms: Mutation.configuration.agent_timeout_ms,
          
      104. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    104. 
            

            

                        neighbors: neighbors
          
      105. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    105. 
            

            

                      }
          
      106. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    106. 
            

            

                    end
          
      107. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    107. 
            

            

                  end
          
      108. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    108. 
            

            

            
          
      109. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    109. 
            

            

                  # Get all agent actions
          
      110. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    110. 
            

            

                  actions = @agent_manager.get_agent_actions_with_individual_states(agent_world_states)
          
      111. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    111. 
            

            

            
          
      112. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    112. 
            

            

                  # Apply actions sequentially to avoid race conditions
          
      113. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    113. 
            

            

                  new_grid = Array.new(@height) { Array.new(@width) { nil } }
          
      114. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    114. 
            

            

            
          
      115. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    115. 
            

            

                  @grid.each_with_index do |row, y|
          
      116. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    116. 
            

            

                    row.each_with_index do |agent, x|
          
      117. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    117. 
            

            

                      next unless agent&.alive
          
      118. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    118. 
            

            

            
          
      119. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    119. 
            

            

                      action = actions[agent.agent_id] || { type: :rest }
          
      120. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    120. 
            

            

                      execute_action(agent, action, x, y, new_grid)
          
      121. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    121. 
            

            

            
          
      122. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    122. 
            

            

                      # Apply energy decay
          
      123. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    123. 
            

            

                      new_energy = agent.energy - Mutation.configuration.energy_decay
          
      124. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    124. 
            

            

                      @agent_manager.update_agent_energy(agent.agent_id, new_energy)
          
      125. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    125. 
            

            

            
          
      126. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    126. 
            

            

                      # Keep agent if still alive
          
      127. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    127. 
            

            

                      if agent.alive && new_energy > 0
          
      128. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    128. 
            

            

                        new_grid[y][x] = agent
          
      129. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    129. 
            

            

                      else
          
      130. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    130. 
            

            

                        @agent_manager.remove_agent(agent.agent_id)
          
      131. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    131. 
            

            

                      end
          
      132. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    132. 
            

            

                    end
          
      133. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    133. 
            

            

                  end
          
      134. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    134. 
            

            

            
          
      135. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    135. 
            

            

                  @grid = new_grid
          
      136. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    136. 
            

            

                  @tick += 1
          
      137. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    137. 
            

            

            
          
      138. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    138. 
            

            

                  update_statistics
          
      139. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    139. 
            

            

                end
          
      140. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    140. 
            

            

            
          
      141. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    141. 
            
              1
            

            

                def execute_action(agent, action, x, y, new_grid)
          
      142. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    142. 
            

            

                  case action[:type]
          
      143. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    143. 
            

            

                  when :attack
          
      144. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    144. 
            

            

                    execute_attack(agent, action[:target], x, y)
          
      145. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    145. 
            

            

                  when :rest
          
      146. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    146. 
            

            

                    execute_rest(agent)
          
      147. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    147. 
            

            

                  when :replicate
          
      148. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    148. 
            

            

                    execute_replicate(agent, x, y, new_grid)
          
      149. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    149. 
            

            

                  when :die
          
      150. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    150. 
            

            

                    agent.die!
          
      151. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    151. 
            

            

                  else
          
      152. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    152. 
            

            

                    execute_rest(agent) # Default action
          
      153. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    153. 
            

            

                  end
          
      154. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    154. 
            

            

                end
          
      155. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    155. 
            

            

            
          
      156. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    156. 
            
              1
            

            

                def execute_attack(agent, target_direction, x, y)
          
      157. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    157. 
            

            

                  target_x, target_y = get_target_position(x, y, target_direction)
          
      158. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    158. 
            

            

                  return unless valid_position?(target_x, target_y)
          
      159. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    159. 
            

            

            
          
      160. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    160. 
            

            

                  target_agent = @grid[target_y][target_x]
          
      161. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    161. 
            

            

                  return unless target_agent&.alive
          
      162. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    162. 
            

            

            
          
      163. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    163. 
            

            

                  # Apply damage
          
      164. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    164. 
            

            

                  damage = Mutation.configuration.attack_damage
          
      165. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    165. 
            

            

                  new_target_energy = target_agent.energy - damage
          
      166. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    166. 
            

            

                  @agent_manager.update_agent_energy(target_agent.agent_id, new_target_energy)
          
      167. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    167. 
            

            

            
          
      168. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    168. 
            

            

                  # Attacker gains energy
          
      169. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    169. 
            

            

                  energy_gain = Mutation.configuration.attack_energy_gain
          
      170. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    170. 
            

            

                  new_attacker_energy = agent.energy + energy_gain
          
      171. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    171. 
            

            

                  @agent_manager.update_agent_energy(agent.agent_id, new_attacker_energy)
          
      172. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    172. 
            

            

            
          
      173. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    173. 
            

            

                  if new_target_energy <= 0
          
      174. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    174. 
            

            

                    @agent_manager.remove_agent(target_agent.agent_id)
          
      175. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    175. 
            

            

                    @grid[target_y][target_x] = nil
          
      176. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    176. 
            

            

                  end
          
      177. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    177. 
            

            

                end
          
      178. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    178. 
            

            

            
          
      179. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    179. 
            
              1
            

            

                def execute_rest(agent)
          
      180. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    180. 
            

            

                  energy_gain = Mutation.configuration.rest_energy_gain
          
      181. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    181. 
            

            

                  new_energy = agent.energy + energy_gain
          
      182. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    182. 
            

            

                  @agent_manager.update_agent_energy(agent.agent_id, new_energy)
          
      183. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    183. 
            

            

                end
          
      184. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    184. 
            

            

            
          
      185. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    185. 
            
              1
            

            

                def execute_replicate(agent, x, y, new_grid)
          
      186. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    186. 
            

            

                  return if agent.energy < Mutation.configuration.replication_cost
          
      187. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    187. 
            

            

            
          
      188. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    188. 
            

            

                  # Population cap to prevent excessive spawning
          
      189. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    189. 
            

            

                  return if agent_count >= @size # Don't exceed grid capacity
          
      190. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    190. 
            

            

            
          
      191. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    191. 
            

            

                  # Find empty adjacent position
          
      192. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    192. 
            

            

                  empty_positions = get_empty_adjacent_positions(x, y)
          
      193. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    193. 
            

            

                  return if empty_positions.empty?
          
      194. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    194. 
            

            

            
          
      195. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    195. 
            

            

                  offspring_x, offspring_y = empty_positions.sample
          
      196. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    196. 
            

            

            
          
      197. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    197. 
            

            

                  # Create offspring with mutation
          
      198. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    198. 
            

            

                  offspring = @agent_manager.create_offspring(agent, offspring_x, offspring_y, @mutation_engine)
          
      199. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    199. 
            

            

                  return unless offspring
          
      200. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    200. 
            

            

            
          
      201. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    201. 
            

            

                  # Subtract replication cost from parent
          
      202. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    202. 
            

            

                  cost = Mutation.configuration.replication_cost
          
      203. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    203. 
            

            

                  new_parent_energy = agent.energy - cost
          
      204. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    204. 
            

            

                  @agent_manager.update_agent_energy(agent.agent_id, new_parent_energy)
          
      205. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    205. 
            

            

            
          
      206. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    206. 
            

            

                  # Place offspring in grid
          
      207. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    207. 
            

            

                  new_grid[offspring_y][offspring_x] = offspring
          
      208. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    208. 
            

            

                  @statistics[:total_agents_created] += 1
          
      209. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    209. 
            

            

                end
          
      210. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    210. 
            

            

            
          
      211. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    211. 
            
              1
            

            

                def get_target_position(x, y, direction)
          
      212. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    212. 
            

            

                  case direction.to_sym
          
      213. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    213. 
            

            

                  when :north then [x, y - 1]
          
      214. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    214. 
            

            

                  when :south then [x, y + 1]
          
      215. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    215. 
            

            

                  when :east then [x + 1, y]
          
      216. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    216. 
            

            

                  when :west then [x - 1, y]
          
      217. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    217. 
            

            

                  when :north_east then [x + 1, y - 1]
          
      218. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    218. 
            

            

                  when :north_west then [x - 1, y - 1]
          
      219. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    219. 
            

            

                  when :south_east then [x + 1, y + 1]
          
      220. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    220. 
            

            

                  when :south_west then [x - 1, y + 1]
          
      221. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    221. 
            

            

                  else [x, y] # Invalid direction
          
      222. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    222. 
            

            

                  end
          
      223. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    223. 
            

            

                end
          
      224. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    224. 
            

            

            
          
      225. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    225. 
            
              1
            

            

                def get_empty_adjacent_positions(x, y)
          
      226. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    226. 
            

            

                  positions = []
          
      227. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    227. 
            

            

                  (-1..1).each do |dx|
          
      228. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    228. 
            

            

                    (-1..1).each do |dy|
          
      229. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    229. 
            

            

                      next if dx == 0 && dy == 0 # Skip center position
          
      230. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    230. 
            

            

                      
          
      231. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    231. 
            

            

                      new_x, new_y = x + dx, y + dy
          
      232. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    232. 
            

            

                      next unless valid_position?(new_x, new_y)
          
      233. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    233. 
            

            

                      next if @grid[new_y][new_x] # Position occupied
          
      234. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    234. 
            

            

                      
          
      235. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    235. 
            

            

                      positions << [new_x, new_y]
          
      236. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    236. 
            

            

                    end
          
      237. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    237. 
            

            

                  end
          
      238. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    238. 
            

            

                  positions
          
      239. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    239. 
            

            

                end
          
      240. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    240. 
            

            

            
          
      241. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    241. 
            
              1
            

            

                def valid_position?(x, y)
          
      242. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    242. 
            

            

                  x >= 0 && x < @width && y >= 0 && y < @height
          
      243. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    243. 
            

            

                end
          
      244. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    244. 
            

            

            
          
      245. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    245. 
            
              1
            

            

                def get_neighbors(x, y)
          
      246. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    246. 
            

            

                  neighbors = []
          
      247. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    247. 
            

            

            
          
      248. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    248. 
            

            

                  # 8-directional neighbors (Moore neighborhood)
          
      249. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    249. 
            

            

                  (-1..1).each do |dy|
          
      250. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    250. 
            

            

                    (-1..1).each do |dx|
          
      251. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    251. 
            

            

                      next if dx == 0 && dy == 0 # Skip center
          
      252. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    252. 
            

            

            
          
      253. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    253. 
            

            

                      neighbor_x = x + dx
          
      254. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    254. 
            

            

                      neighbor_y = y + dy
          
      255. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    255. 
            

            

            
          
      256. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    256. 
            

            

                      if neighbor_x >= 0 && neighbor_x < @width && neighbor_y >= 0 && neighbor_y < @height
          
      257. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    257. 
            

            

                        neighbors << @grid[neighbor_y][neighbor_x]
          
      258. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    258. 
            

            

                      else
          
      259. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    259. 
            

            

                        neighbors << nil # Outside world boundary
          
      260. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    260. 
            

            

                      end
          
      261. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    261. 
            

            

                    end
          
      262. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    262. 
            

            

                  end
          
      263. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    263. 
            

            

            
          
      264. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    264. 
            

            

                  neighbors
          
      265. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    265. 
            

            

                end
          
      266. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    266. 
            

            

            
          
      267. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    267. 
            
              1
            

            

                def living_agents
          
      268. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    268. 
            

            

                  @agent_manager.living_agents
          
      269. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    269. 
            

            

                end
          
      270. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    270. 
            

            

            
          
      271. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    271. 
            
              1
            

            

                def agent_count
          
      272. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    272. 
            

            

                  living_agents.count
          
      273. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    273. 
            

            

                end
          
      274. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    274. 
            

            

            
          
      275. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    275. 
            
              1
            

            

                def all_dead?
          
      276. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    276. 
            

            

                  agent_count == 0
          
      277. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    277. 
            

            

                end
          
      278. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    278. 
            

            

            
          
      279. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    279. 
            
              1
            

            

                def average_energy
          
      280. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    280. 
            

            

                  agents = living_agents

                    agent_actions.each do |agent_data|

                    @grid = new_grid

                    @tick += 1

                    update_statistics

                  {

                def get_neighbors(x, y)

                def execute_action(agent, action, x, y, new_grid)

                  case action

                def execute_attack(agent, x, y)
          
      200. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    200. 
            

            

                  target_x, target_y = find_attack_target(x, y)
          
      201. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    201. 
            

            

                  return unless target_x && target_y
          
      202. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    202. 
            

            

            
          
      203. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    203. 
            

            

                  target = @grid[target_y][target_x]
          
      204. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    204. 
            

            

                  return unless target&.alive?
          
      205. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    205. 
            

            

            
          
      206. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    206. 
            

            

                  damage = Mutation.configuration.attack_damage

                  gain = Mutation.configuration.attack_energy_gain
          
      208.

                  target.energy -= damage
          
      210.

                  agent.energy += gain
          
      211. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    211. 
            

            

            
          
      212.

                  Mutation.logger.debug("Agent #{agent.id} attacked #{target.id} at (#{target_x},#{target_y}) for #{damage} damage")
          
      213.

                end

                def execute_replication(agent, x, y, new_grid)
          
      223. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    223. 
            

            

                  return unless agent.energy >= Mutation.configuration.replication_cost
          
      224. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    224. 
            

            

            
          
      225. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    225. 
            

            

                  empty_x, empty_y = find_empty_adjacent_position(x, y)
          
      226.

                  return unless empty_x && empty_y
          
      227. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    227.

                  cost = Mutation.configuration.replication_cost

      230.

                  new_grid[empty_y][empty_x] = offspring

                  @statistics[:total_agents_created] += 1

    234.

                  Mutation.logger.debug("Agent #{agent.id} replicated at (#{empty_x},#{empty_y}), created #{offspring.id}")

                end

                def find_attack_target(x, y)
          
      239.

                  candidates = []

                  (-1..1).each do |dy|
          
      243. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    243. 
            

            

                    (-1..1).each do |dx|
          
      244. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    244. 
            

            

                      next if dx.zero? && dy.zero? # Skip center cell

      249.

      250.

                  end
          
      251.

                  return nil if candidates.empty?
          
      253.

      254.

                  # Attack the neighbor with highest energy
          
      255.
